          <msContents>
            <msItem n="1" defective="true">
              <locus from="58v" to="62v">58v-62v</locus>
              <title>Drauma-Jóns saga</title>
              <incipit defective="true">HEinrekr er maðr nefndr jarll at tign </incipit>
              <explicit defective="true">siðan bruðlaups timi þeira keisarara systur var vm geingin
                er gerðizst með</explicit>
              <note>Approximately 80 words are missing from the end of the saga.</note>
              <textLang mainLang="isl">Icelandic</textLang> <!-- OEH 2022-10-11: Added this line, useful for the display of the text in the Menota catalogue  -->
            </msItem>

          <physDesc>
            <objectDesc facs="codex">
              <supportDesc>
                <support>
                  <p><material>Parchment</material></p>
                </support>
                <extent>100 leaves; 222 mm (height) by 173 mm (width)</extent>
                <foliation><p>Each leaf is numbered twice, on the recto side: an older collation
                    numbering in black ink in the upper right-hand corner, and a later pencil
                    numbering in the top margin.</p></foliation>
                <condition><p>The manuscript is in reasonably good condition.</p>
                  <p>Folio <locus from="60r" to="60v">60</locus> has the most damage with a cut and
                    fold affecting the top line of both sides, and a significant piece cut from the
                    bottom margin next to the spine, resulting in damage to the last two lines on
                    each side. A vertical fold line also runs down the middle of the page and causes
                    further reading difficulties, more so on the verso side, especially at the top
                    and bottom of the page. Damage and fading near the spine on the bottom third of
                    the page also poses problems interpreting the end of each line.</p>
                  <p><locus from="62r" to="62r">62r</locus> has similar vertical line fold damage
                    but has less impact on readability; a horizontal cut along line 1, however,
                    makes some words difficult to distinguish.</p>
                </condition>
              </supportDesc>
              <layoutDesc>
                <layout columns="1" writtenLines="33">
                  <p>The text is written in one column of 33 lines; there are approximately 12-16
                    words per line.</p>
                </layout>
              </layoutDesc>
            </objectDesc>
            <handDesc hands="1">
              <handNote scope="major" scribe="IV" script="árléttiskrift">The saga was written by a
                single unidentified scribe. Four separate hands can be distinguished in the
                manuscript as a whole.</handNote>
            </handDesc>
            <decoDesc>
              <decoNote type="initial">
                <p>Fol. <locus from="58v" to="58v">58v:6-58v:22</locus>: Major pen flourished
                  initial H in blue and red, with red infill, and blue and red external pen flourish
                  extending into the margin and spanning lines 6 to 22.</p>
              </decoNote>
              <decoNote type="paratext">
                <p>Fol. <locus from="58v" to="58v">58v:10</locus>: The rubric “af drauma joni” is
                  written in red ink at the end of the opening line; it is followed on the same line
                  by the second half of the final word of the preceding text.</p>
              </decoNote>
            </decoDesc>
            <additions>
              <p>Written In Icelandic at the bottom of fol. <locus from="62v" to="62v">62v</locus>
                in a different, later hand is: vantar 2 blǫð</p>
            </additions>
            <accMat><p>At the back of the manuscript are ten loose leaves (pp. 91-100), which for a
                time belonged to AM 764 b 4to.</p><p>There is an AM note.</p>
            </accMat>
          </physDesc>
          <history>
            <origin>
              <p>Written in <origPlace key="IS">Iceland</origPlace>. Kålund (Kålund: Catalog vol. II
                p. 68) has dated it to the <origDate notBefore="1350" notAfter="1399">14th
                  century</origDate>. However, Unger (Heilagra Manna søgur vol. I p. Xv), and later
                Jakobsen (Studier i Clarus saga p. 12) and Louis-Jensen ("Enoks saga") dated it to
                approx. 1375</p>
            </origin>
          </history>
        </msDesc>
      </sourceDesc>
    </fileDesc>

        <p>This encoding follows the standard set out in <title>The Menota Handbook</title> (version

            http://www.menota.org/handbook</ref> as of <date>2019-05-10</date>.</p>

          manuscript.</p>
      </projectDesc>
      <editorialDecl>
        <correction status="high">
          <p>This text has been transcribed directly from photographic colour facsimiles of the
            manuscript.</p>
          <p>The text was proofread by <name type="person">Philip Knight</name> and colleagues
            before publication in 2022. It is unlikely to contain a significant number of errors,
            though some errors cannot be ruled out.</p>
        </correction>
        <normalization me:level="facs dipl norm">
